# Master Build Completion Plan

## Purpose

This file is the authoritative repo-truth completion plan for the currently exposed Selene build scope:

- Build Sections 01 through 11
- APP_IPHONE
- APP_MAC_DESKTOP

It may only be updated from current repo truth, exact command results, and exact file-and-line evidence. If repo truth is not explicit, the correct value is `NOT_EXPLICIT`, not inference. The detailed checkoff ledger lives in [MASTER_BUILD_COMPLETION_LEDGER.md](/Users/selene/Documents/Selene-OS/docs/MASTER_BUILD_COMPLETION_LEDGER.md).

- Canonical Stage 3A provider safety update: `STAGE_3A_PROVIDER_SECRET_KMS_COST_QUOTA_VAULT_PROVIDER_OFF_PROOF_AND_EARLY_CONSENT_BASELINE_RECONCILIATION` closes the narrowed provider/KMS/cost/quota/provider-off/early-consent foundation needed before Stage 4 packet work. Existing `PH1.KMS`, `provider_secrets`, `PH1.COST`, `PH1.QUOTA`, `PH1.PROVIDERCTL`, runtime bootstrap health/readiness/startup behavior, vault CLI surfaces, and PH1.F storage remain the repo-truth carriers. Stage 3A adds the minimal `ConsentStatePacket` / `ConsentScope` / `ConsentDecisionState` contract and PH1.F `ConsentStateRepo` append-only storage/current lookup path. Provider-off proof shows zero attempts and zero network dispatches, startup probes remain disabled before provider use, and health/startup endpoints do not fetch provider secrets. Broad model/provider championship routing remains deferred to Stage 3B/Stage 30. Stage 4A is ready to start as activation/session/turn packet reconciliation.
- Canonical Stage 2A foundation update: `STAGE_2A_RUNTIME_KERNEL_STORAGE_PROOF_LEDGER_LAW_AND_MINIMAL_BENCHMARK_ENVELOPE_RECONCILIATION` closes the narrowed Stage 2 foundation. Existing runtime/kernel/storage/proof/law carriers remain the repo-truth foundation; canonical packet names that are roadmap aliases are crosswalked instead of duplicated. The minimal benchmark envelope now exists as PH1.J `BenchmarkTargetPacket` / `BenchmarkResultPacket` contracts, `BenchmarkTargetStatus` / `BenchmarkComparisonOutcome` statuses, and a PH1.F-backed `BenchmarkResultRepo` append-only target/result storage path with idempotency, by-target lookup, latest-result lookup, and result-to-target certification comparison. Stage 3A is ready to start as provider/KMS/cost/provider-off/early-consent reconciliation.
- Desktop search visual parity and real image-card repair update: `DESKTOP_SEARCH_VISUAL_PARITY_REAL_ENTITY_IMAGES_AND_FULL_VOICE_SMOKE_BUILD_V3` adds the final visual-search law, keeps Desktop renderer-only, tightens approved remote image-card transport, and improves ChatGPT-style source-pill placement/style without making Desktop search/rank/choose images. PH1.E now supports generic public role/entity search query expansion, generic trailing-location qualifier stripping, accepted-source-only image augmentation from the controlled Brave image metadata path, stronger wrong-entity and thin-directory rejection, and person-name extraction around role claims without real searched-name or company-specific patches. Kernel contracts and adapter transport now admit policy-approved remote image cards only when the source page is safe, `display_allowed=true`, remote image loading is explicitly allowed, and image metadata stays out of `response_text`/`tts_text`. Desktop decodes approved image cards, renders actual approved images/thumbnails with placeholder only for loading/failure, and renders compact clickable source pills below authoritative replies.
- Offline entity-role search quality repair update: `OFFLINE_ENTITY_ROLE_SEARCH_QUALITY_REPAIR` repairs the synthetic/fake-provider backend lane before any new live Brave or Desktop voice proof. PH1.E now preserves additional generic role aliases such as chief executive officer, president, and head-of role forms in entity-role extraction and role-aware query planning, and closest-supported public role answers can carry approved fixture image cards from accepted source metadata without treating image metadata as factual proof. Exact source-backed roles answer directly, exact-role-missing cases return the closest supported accepted-source role, weak/thin directory evidence remains rejected, wrong-entity evidence remains rejected, accepted source chips attach to the answer, and `response_text`/`tts_text` stay free of confidence labels, raw URLs, rejected-source details, and image metadata.
- Offline entity-role proof status: no live Brave, live image provider, provider key inspection, Desktop launch, or Desktop voice proof was run by design. Verification passed for `cargo check -p selene_os -p selene_adapter -p selene_engines`; targeted `role`, `source`, `image`, and `best_available` filters across `selene_engines`, `selene_os`, and `selene_adapter` where present; full `cargo test -p selene_adapter -- --test-threads=1 => lib 276 passed; 4 ignored plus bins/integration`, full `cargo test -p selene_os -- --test-threads=1 => lib 1377 passed plus bins/doc-tests`, full `cargo test -p selene_engines -- --test-threads=1 => 648 passed; 12 ignored`; `git diff --check`; leak scan with remaining hits classified as tests, fixture parser, contracts, or non-user-facing trace; and forbidden real-name scan with no matches outside docs/target. `xcodebuild` was not run because no Desktop/Swift packet shape changed. Next build remains controlled live Brave entity proof, followed by real Desktop voice proof after typed/live entity quality passes.
- Desktop search visual parity proof status: synthetic image/source-chip tests and full Rust verification pass, provider-off proof after live testing passes, and the Brave key was present without being printed. Controlled live Brave typed probes remained under the JD cap and exposed a remaining live search-quality blocker: real entity/company role prompts safe-degraded rather than proving a source-backed CEO/person-photo answer, so live real-image answer proof is `NOT_PROVEN`. The explicit Desktop UI/voice phase launched the app and attempted a no-search English mic smoke with synthetic speaker-to-mic audio; intended `Explain what Selene is.` was captured as `Explain what Celine is.`, so the prompt is invalid for voice proof and exposes a voice/STT assistant-name ambiguity blocker. Chinese Desktop microphone proof was not run after that invalidating mismatch. Typed/runtime proof is not counted as voice proof. Readiness for this visual build is therefore `BLOCKED_BY_SEARCH_QUALITY` plus `READY_EXCEPT_REAL_VOICE_NOT_PROVEN` until the live provider/source-ranking path returns accepted sources and approved images for public entity queries and the real Desktop mic path captures valid English/Chinese transcripts.
- Best available public search answer policy update: `SEARCH_BEST_AVAILABLE_ANSWER_POLICY_AND_CONFLICT_RESOLUTION_REPAIR` repairs the post-Stage 9 public websearch answer policy so accepted-source conflict no longer ends as a generic empty-handed conflict answer. PH1.E now distinguishes exact support from closest source-backed support, selects the clearest accepted source for mixed evidence with a natural caveat, returns closest supported role/title information when the exact requested role is absent, and keeps stale evidence useful but clearly non-current. PH1.X fallback wording now returns the closest search result without raw snippets/URLs when verification metadata is absent, while user-facing `response_text`/`tts_text` remain free of confidence labels, internal classes, raw provider payloads, source dumps, and rejected-source details. Desktop source chips now render as compact clickable source pills directly under the authoritative reply text and in provenance, matching the required small-source-link behavior without making Desktop provider-authoritative.
- Best available answer implementation proof points: AGENTS.md now contains the `Best Available Public Search Answer` law; PH1.E implements closest-support and mixed-evidence answer selection in [ph1e.rs](/Users/selene/Documents/Selene-OS/crates/selene_engines/src/ph1e.rs); additive kernel contract tokens for closest/mixed/stale answer classes and closest evidence support live in [ph1e.rs](/Users/selene/Documents/Selene-OS/crates/selene_kernel_contracts/src/ph1e.rs); PH1.X same-language/fallback presentation lives in [ph1x.rs](/Users/selene/Documents/Selene-OS/crates/selene_os/src/ph1x.rs); adapter regressions prove best-available source-truth behavior in [lib.rs](/Users/selene/Documents/Selene-OS/crates/selene_adapter/src/lib.rs); compact Desktop source pills live in [DesktopSessionShellView.swift](/Users/selene/Documents/Selene-OS/apple/mac_desktop/SeleneMacDesktop/DesktopSessionShellView.swift). Protected execution remains simulation/authority gated and cannot use best-available guessing.

1. Confirm branch, local HEAD, remote HEAD, and clean-tree truth with exact git command output.
2. Run the readiness audit and the targeted carrier tests for the touched workstream.
3. Update the relevant section summary, blocker map, winner-chain note, and next-safe-scope ordering only if new repo truth changes them.
4. Update only the affected ledger rows using exact file-and-line evidence and exact command results.
5. If repo truth is still silent on a criterion, leave it as `NOT_EXPLICIT`.
6. If a criterion is only partially live, leave it `PARTIAL` until code plus test or audit evidence prove completion.

## Check-Off Rule

Nothing in this plan or in the companion ledger may be marked complete unless repo truth proves it with:

- exact file-and-line evidence
- exact test or audit evidence
- canonical separation truth showing whether the evidence is `CANONICAL_LIVE_RUNTIME`, `APP_LAYER_ONLY`, `TEST_ONLY`, or `DOC_ONLY`

If one of those proof elements is missing, the correct ledger state is `PARTIAL`, `BLOCKED`, `NOT_STARTED`, or `NOT_EXPLICIT`, never silent completion.

Existing runtime ingress/session carriers were preserved and not rebuilt. `Stage4ActivationPacket`, `Stage4ActivationSource`, `Stage4TurnBoundaryPacket`, `Stage4TurnBoundaryKind`, `Stage4RecordBoundary`, `Stage4RecordingState`, and `Stage4PacketRouteAuthority` now provide the minimal activation/session/turn packet-boundary proof in `crates/selene_os/src/runtime_ingress_turn_foundation.rs`. Packet creation has explicit no-authority proof for tools, search, providers, TTS, and protected execution. Record-button packets remain artifact-only and cannot carry live turn, route, modality, or device turn sequence state. Wake detection, STT/TTS, Voice ID matching, native UI, and the full record-mode product remain deferred to their owning stages. Stage 5A is ready to start as session open/resume/close, runtime turn spine, and stale-turn quarantine reconciliation.

Append-only canonical Stage 5A implementation update (2026-05-03): `STAGE_5A_SESSION_OPEN_RESUME_CLOSE_RUNTIME_TURN_SPINE_AND_STALE_TURN_QUARANTINE_RECONCILIATION` completed the narrowed session/turn authority proof after Stage 4A. Existing PH1.L and `RuntimeSessionFoundation` session lifecycle carriers were preserved and not rebuilt. `Stage5TurnAuthorityPacket`, `Stage5TurnAuthorityDisposition`, and `Stage5TurnWorkAuthority` now provide the minimal current-turn authority and stale-result quarantine carrier in `crates/selene_os/src/runtime_session_foundation.rs`; `authorize_stage5_current_committed_turn` proves a committed turn can enter later understanding only when it matches the session permit, active device timeline, current device sequence, non-closed session state, and no newer deferred/committed turn. Stale, superseded, cancelled, abandoned, closed-session, and record-artifact-only dispositions cannot enter understanding, render as the current answer, or route tools, search, providers, TTS, connector work, or protected execution. Record sessions remain distinct from live chat through the Stage 4A record boundary plus the Stage 5A `RecordArtifactOnly` quarantine disposition. Broad conversation-control, clarification, correction, recovery, same-page state, and natural turn-taking/backchannel behavior remain deferred to Stage 5B. Stage 5B is required before broad Stage 5 is complete.
